611→\tsubpath := route.Param(ctx, \"subpath\")\n   612→\n   613→\tif subpath == \"/pprof\" {\n   614→\t\thttp.Redirect(w, req, req.URL.Path+\"/\", http.StatusMovedPermanently)\n   615→\t\treturn\n   616→\t}\n   617→\n   618→\tif !strings.HasPrefix(subpath, \"/pprof/\") {\n   619→\t\thttp.NotFound(w, req)\n   620→\t\treturn\n   621→\t}\n   622→\tsubpath = strings.TrimPrefix(subpath, \"/pprof/\")\n   623→\n   624→\tswitch subpath {\n   625→\tcase \"cmdline\":\n   626→\t\tpprof.Cmdline(w, req)\n   627→\tcase \"profile\":\n   628→\t\tpprof.Profile(w, req)\n   629→\tcase \"symbol\":\n   630→\t\tpprof.Symbol(w, req)\n   631→\tcase \"trace\":\n   632→\t\tpprof.Trace(w, req)\n   633→\tcase \"fgprof\":\n   634→\t\tfgprofHandler.ServeHTTP(w, req)\n   635→\tdefault:\n   636→\t\treq.URL.Path = \"/debug/pprof/\" + subpath\n   637→\t\tpprof.Index(w, req)\n   638→\t}\n   639→}\n   640→\n   641→// SetReady sets the ready status of our web Handler.\n   642→func (h *Handler) SetReady(v ReadyStatus) {\n   643→\tif v == Ready {\n   644→\t\th.ready.Store(uint32(Ready))\n   645→\t\th.metrics.readyStatus.Set(1)\n   646→\t\treturn\n   647→\t}\n   648→\n   649→\th.ready.Store(uint32(v))\n   650→\th.metrics.readyStatus.Set(0)\n   651→}\n   652→\n   653→// Verifies whether the server is ready or not.\n   654→func (h *Handler) isReady() bool {\n   655→\treturn ReadyStatus(h.ready.Load()) == Ready\n   656→}\n   657→\n   658→// Checks if server is ready, calls f if it is, returns 503 if it is not.\n   659→func (h *Handler) testReady(f (api_v1.RuntimeInfo, error) {\n\tstatus := api_v1.RuntimeInfo{\n\t\tStartTime:      h.birth,\n\t\tCWD:            h.cwd,\n\t\tGoroutineCount: runtime.NumGoroutine(),\n\t\tGOMAXPROCS:
